  category_name STRING
);

CREATE TABLE orders (
  order_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
  order_date DATE,
  product_id INT,
  quantity INT,
  FOREIGN KEY (product_id) REFERENCES products(product_id)
);

CREATE TABLE suppliers (
  supplier_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
  supplier_name STRING,
  supplier_contact STRING
);
